 rajasthan kaa naam sunate hi jehan main ret ke tilon, shandaar kilon, sundar nartakon, lokgeeton or utsavon kii chhavi ubhar aati he
 Most of these images are not unrealistic
 aaj bhi rajasthan main inke najaare dikh jaaenge
 But the images of its history, heritage and cultural identity are even greater
 pracheen khandhiron main aisi bhi jagahen hai, jahaan isa purv teesri shatadbradi ke eent-gaare ke bhawan vaale nagar, sidhe mudati sadaken or nalee-naalon kii vyavastha mil jaaegi
 These cities belong to the 'harappan civilization' period
 aise kareeb 25 sthal uttar or uttar-pashchim rajasthan main ghagghar-hakaraa nadi ghati main paae gaye hai
 Prominent among these are Kalibanga, Pilibanga and Sothi etc
 isi tarah dakshin-purvi rajasthan main banaas or uski sahaayak nadiyon kii ghati main kareeb nabbe sthal tamba-utpaadak ahaad sabhyataa ke hai
 Along with this, there are also structures of pre-mauryan and Mauryan period
 inamen buddha stupa or math bairaat nagari, chittorgadh or lalsot main paae gaye
 Bairat (now called Viratnagar) near Alwar has the ruins of a circular Buddhist stupa surrounded by wooden pillars
 iske paas hi khudaai se ek buddha math kaa pataa chalaa he, jisamen chabutare or kothriyaan hai
 Two inscriptions inscribed in Brahmi script are also found in Bairat
 inamen ek 'baurat shilaalekh' ab kolkata kii aciatic socity main he or doosraa samraat ashok ke 'laghu shilaalekh' jaisaa he

 duusare pracheen aitihaasik sthal isa purv teesri shatabdi se isvi san chauthi shatabdi tak ke hai

 It was called Narayana Vatika
 raidh ke khandhar pracheen malwa raaj ke hai
 There are three small brick houses in them

 The importance of naliyasar-sambhar dates from the first century to the 11th century
 vahaan yojana ke anuroop sadaken or do se teen manjila eent ke makaan milte hai
 The Gupta Empire spread to many parts of South Asia between 350‚Äì400 CE
 isse rajasthan kii vaastukala bhi prabhavit hui or pathar ke bhawanon par minar kii tarah kaa shikhar rajasthan kii mandir parampara kaa hissaa ho gaya
 The temples at Mukundara Dara near Kota in Rajasthan, the Bhurmar Mata Temple at Chhoti Sadi near Chittorgarh in the 5th century and the Charchaima temple at Kota are examples of Gupta period architecture
 gupt kaal kii vaastukala uttar-gupt kaal main bhi prachlit rahi, jaisaa ki rajasthan ke dakshin-purvi ilaake main jagat, thanesar, kalyanpur, amajhera, nagda, samauli or jhalawad ilaake main kholvi, binnayaga or hathiyagaur ke pathar katkar banaae mandiron main dikhataa he
 The ancient city of Chandravati in Jhalrapatan near Jhalawar is an important example of 7th-12th century regional art and architecture
 8veen-11veen sadi main uttar bharat ke bade hisse main vishaal samrajya sthapit karne vaale gurjar-pratihaar raajaaon ne uttar-gupt kaal main is kshetra kii vaastukala parampara ko prabhavit kiya
 The 8th century renovated Kalika Mata temple of Chittorgarh is a specimen of the gurjara-parihara style
 is kaal main kai nagaron or prashaskeey thikaanon kaa vikaas hua
 Many dynasties built new settlements or new cities in them

 Giri Durg and Dhanva Durg were also built here
 inamen kai rajwanshon ke badal jane ke baad bhi sthaneey raajaaon kii rajdhaniyaan or vyapaar centre pehle kii tarah bane rahe
 Rajasthan has a tradition of change in the 17th and 18th centuries
 jaipur kaa nayaa shahar bana
